FROM (
    SELECT s.name, s.city, s.house_number, s.postal_code, s.region, s.street_name
    FROM storage AS s
    WHERE s.name = @__name_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS s2
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT s0.product_name, s0.storage_name, s0.count, s0.minimal_count, p.product_name AS product_name0, p.last_price, p.unit_code, p0.unit_code AS unit_code0, p0.unit_name

    SELECT s.name, s.city, s.house_number, s.postal_code, s.region, s.street_name
    FROM storage AS s
    WHERE s.name = @__name_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS s2
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT s0.product_name, s0.storage_name, s0.count, s0.minimal_count, p.product_name AS product_name0, p.last_price, p.unit_code, p0.unit_code AS unit_code0, p0.unit_name

    INNER JOIN product AS p ON s0.product_name = p.product_name
    INNER JOIN product_units AS p0 ON p.unit_code = p0.unit_code
) AS s3 ON s2.name = s3.storage_name

2025-05-03 23:46:02.614 +03:00 [INF] (Microsoft.EntityFrameworkCore.Database.Command) Executed DbCommand (22ms) [Parameters=[@__name_0='?'], CommandType='"Text"', CommandTimeout='30']
SELECT s2.name, s2.city, s2.house_number, s2.postal_code, s2.region, s2.street_name, s3.product_name, s3.storage_name, s3.count, s3.minimal_count, s3.product_name0, s3.last_price, s3.unit_code, s3.unit_code0, s3.unit_name, s1.phone_number, s1.email, s1.first_name, s1.last_name, s1.storage_name, s1.user_id
FROM (
    SELECT s.name, s.city, s.house_number, s.postal_code, s.region, s.street_name
    FROM storage AS s
    WHERE s.name = @__name_0
    LIMIT 1
) AS s2
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT s0.product_name, s0.storage_name, s0.count, s0.minimal_count, p.product_name AS product_name0, p.last_price, p.unit_code, p0.unit_code AS unit_code0, p0.unit_name
    FROM storage_product AS s0
    INNER JOIN product AS p ON s0.product_name = p.product_name
    INNER JOIN product_units AS p0 ON p.unit_code = p0.unit_code
) AS s3 ON s2.name = s3.storage_name
LEFT JOIN storage_keeper AS s1 ON s2.name = s1.storage_name
ORDER BY s2.name, s3.product_name, s3.storage_name, s3.product_name0, s3.unit_code0
